6930,STOCKHOLM_SOL,SWEDEN,+59:21:00,+018:04:12,30 m 
----------------------------------------------------------------
* Land use:

* Soil type:

* Surface coverage:

* History:
The measuring site for global radiation and sunshine duration has moved a couple of times within Stockholm. The maximum distance is about 7 km between Bromma – Stocksund and between Bromma – Royal Institute of Technology (KTH). The present site at KTH is located about 3.5 km from Stocksund and 3 km from Fridhemsplan. Details are in https://www.smhi.se/publikationer/publikationer/long-term-global-radiation-in-stockholm-1922-2018-1.145705
